       \'featured\' => false,\n    ), $atts);\n\n    $args = array(\n        \'post_type\' => \'package\',\n        \'posts_per_page\' => $atts[\'limit\'],\n    );\n\n    if ($atts[\'featured\']) {\n        $args[\'meta_key\'] = \'featured_package\';\n        $args[\'meta_value\'] = 1;\n    }\n\n    $packages = new WP_Query($args);\n    $output = \'<div class="packages-grid">\';\n\n    if ($packages->have_posts()) {\n        while ($packages->have_posts()) {\n            $packages->the_post();\n            ob_start();\n            get_template_part(\'template-parts/package-card\');\n            $output .= ob_get_clean();\n        }\n    }\n\n    $output .= \'</div>\';\n    wp_reset_postdata();\n\n    return $output;\n}\nadd_shortcode(\'package_grid\', \'arsyila_package_grid_shortcode\');\n```\n\n---\n\n## âš™ï¸ Functions & Hooks\n\n### Theme Setup\n\n```php\nfunction arsyila_theme_setup() {\n    // Theme support\n    add_theme_support(\'title-tag\');\n    add_theme_support(\'post-thumbnails\');\n    add_theme_support(\'html5\', array(\'search-form\', \'comment-form\', \'gallery\', \'caption\'));\n    \n    // Image sizes\n    add_image_size(\'package-thumb\', 400, 300, true);\n    add_image_size(\'package-large\', 800, 600, true);\n    \n    // Load text domain\n    load_theme_textdomain(\'arsyila-tours\', get_template_directory() . \'/languages\');\n}\nadd_action(\'after_setup_theme\', \'arsyila_theme_setup\');\n```\n\n### Enqueue Scripts & Styles\n\n```php\nfunction arsyila_enqueue_scripts() {\n    wp_enqueue_style(\'arsyila-styles\', get_template_directory_uri() . \'/assets/css/styles.css\', array(), \'1.0.0\');\n    \n    wp_enqueue_script(\'arsyila-scripts\', get_template_directory_uri() . \'/assets/js/main.js\', array(\'jquery\'), \'1.0.0\', true);\n    \n    // Pass data to JavaScript\n    wp_localize_script(\'arsyila-scripts\', \'arsyilaData\', array(\n        \'ajaxUrl\' => admin_url(\'admin-ajax.php\'),\n        \'nonce\' => wp_create_nonce(\'arsyila-nonce\'),\n    ));\n}\nadd_action(\'wp_enqueue_scripts\', \'arsyila_enqueue_scripts\');\n```\n\n---\n\n## ðŸš€ Custom Fields (ACF) Pro\n   - CPT UI (optional, if you prefer UI instead of code)\n   - Contact Form 7 (for booking form)\n\n3. **Import ACF Fields**\n   - Copy the ACF field groups to `inc/acf-fields.php`\n   - Or use ACF\'s import/export feature\n\n4. **Set Up Pages**\n   - Create pages: Home, Packages, Booking, Payment\n   - Assign templates from Page Attributes\n\n5. **Configure Conversion\n\n1. **Use WordPress Functions**\n   - Replace hardcoded text with `the_field()`, `get_field()`\n   - Use `wp_get_attachment_image_src()` for images\n   - Use `get_permalink()` for links\n\n2. **Maintain CSS Structure**\n   - Keep existing CSS classes\n   - Use `body_class()` for page-specific styling\n   - Add WordPress-specific classes\n\n3. **Optimize Performance**\n   - Use `wp_enqueue_scripts` for CSS/JS\n   - Implement lazy loading for images\n   - Use WordPress caching plugins\n\n4. **Security**\n   - Always escape output: `esc_html()`, `esc_url()`, `esc_attr()`\n   - Use `wp_nonce_field()` for forms\n   - Sanitize input: `sanitize_text_field()`, `sanitize_email()`\n\n---\n\n**For questions or support, contact the development
